
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Analyze the properties of the convex equilateral hexagon with opposite sides parallel to establish geometric constraints.'}, {'objective': 'Determine the relationship between the triangle formed by the extensions of sides AB, CD, and EF and the hexagon.'}, {'objective': "Formulate equations relating the triangle's side lengths to the hexagon's side length using parallelism and similarity."}, {'objective': 'Solve the equations to find the side length of the hexagon.'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- The figure is a convex equilateral hexagon ABCDEF, meaning all its sides have equal length.
- All pairs of opposite sides are parallel, implying ABCDEF is a parallelogon with three pairs of parallel sides.
- A triangle is formed by the extensions of sides AB, CD, and EF; the side lengths of this triangle are given as 200, 240, and 300.
- The objective is to find the common side length of the hexagon.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- Since ABCDEF is equilateral and has opposite sides parallel, it is a special type of hexagon often called an equilateral parallelogon.
- The triangle formed by the extensions of AB, CD, and EF likely corresponds to the triangle formed by the intersection points of the lines containing these sides.
- The side lengths 200, 240, and 300 of this triangle relate to the directions and spacing of the hexagon’s sides.
- The parallelism and equal length conditions impose strong geometric constraints, linking the hexagon’s side length to the triangle’s side lengths.
- Understanding how the triangle’s sides correspond to the hexagon’s geometry is key to relating the given lengths.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies primarily in Euclidean geometry, specifically polygon geometry.
- Subfields include convex polygons, properties of parallelogons, and geometric constructions involving parallel lines and side lengths.
- Such problems are common in mathematical competitions and advanced geometry studies.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The exact construction of the triangle from the extensions of AB, CD, and EF is not explicitly described; it is assumed to be the triangle formed by the intersection of the lines containing these sides.
- The orientation and labeling of the hexagon’s vertices are not specified, which might affect the interpretation of opposite sides.
- It is assumed the hexagon is convex and equilateral with the stated parallelism, but no information on angles or coordinates is given.
- The problem assumes uniqueness of the hexagon’s side length given the triangle’s side lengths, which may require justification.
- To proceed, one might assume standard orientation and that the triangle is formed by the intersection points of the extended lines of AB, CD, and EF.

async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_agent = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)

    cot_sc_agents = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(self.max_sc)]

    reflexion_cot_agent = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    reflexion_critic_agent = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)

    debate_agents = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Debate Agent", model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.5) for role in self.debate_role]

    # Stage 0

    cot_instruction_1 = "Sub-task 1: Formally define the geometric properties of the hexagon ABCDEF: establish that it is convex, equilateral (all sides equal), and that opposite sides are parallel, identifying the pairs (AB//DE, BC//EF, CD//FA)."
    subtask_desc_1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent([taskInfo], cot_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, defining hexagon properties, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    subtask_desc_1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking1, "answer": answer1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_instruction_2 = "Sub-task 2: Represent the hexagon sides as vectors and express the parallelism and equilateral conditions in vector form, including the relationship that the sum of the six side vectors is zero (closed polygon)."
    subtask_desc_2 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking2, answer2 = await cot_agent([taskInfo, thinking1], cot_instruction_2, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, vector representation of hexagon, thinking: {thinking2.content}; answer: {answer2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")
    subtask_desc_2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking2, "answer": answer2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_2)
    print("Step 2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_3 = "Sub-task 3: Clarify the construction of the triangle formed by the extensions of sides AB, CD, and EF: identify the triangle as formed by the intersection points of the lines containing these sides and describe how its side lengths relate to the hexagon's geometry."
    subtask_desc_3 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_3",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_3,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    possible_answers_3 = []
    possible_thinkings_3 = []
    for i in range(self.max_sc):
        thinking3, answer3 = await cot_sc_agents[i]([taskInfo, thinking1], cot_sc_instruction_3, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_sc_agents[i].id}, clarifying triangle construction, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}")
        possible_answers_3.append(answer3)
        possible_thinkings_3.append(thinking3)

    final_decision_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking3, answer3 = await final_decision_agent_3([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_3, "Sub-task 3: Synthesize and choose the most consistent answer for triangle construction." , is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}")
    subtask_desc_3['response'] = {"thinking": thinking3, "answer": answer3}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_3)
    print("Step 3: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Stage 1

    cot_instruction_4 = "Sub-task 4: Express the directions of the lines containing AB, CD, and EF in terms of the hexagon side vectors and determine the angles between these lines using the parallelism conditions."
    subtask_desc_4 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_4",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_4,
        "context": ["user query", thinking2.content, thinking3.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking4, answer4 = await cot_agent([taskInfo, thinking2, thinking3], cot_instruction_4, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, analyzing directions and angles, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}")
    subtask_desc_4['response'] = {"thinking": thinking4, "answer": answer4}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_4)
    print("Step 4: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_5 = "Sub-task 5: Relate the side lengths of the triangle formed by the extensions (200, 240, 300) to the distances between the intersection points of the lines containing AB, CD, and EF, using geometric or vector methods."
    subtask_desc_5 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_5",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_5,
        "context": ["user query", thinking3.content, thinking4.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    possible_answers_5 = []
    possible_thinkings_5 = []
    for i in range(self.max_sc):
        thinking5, answer5 = await cot_sc_agents[i]([taskInfo, thinking3, thinking4], cot_sc_instruction_5, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_sc_agents[i].id}, relating triangle side lengths, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}")
        possible_answers_5.append(answer5)
        possible_thinkings_5.append(thinking5)

    final_decision_agent_5 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking5, answer5 = await final_decision_agent_5([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_5, "Sub-task 5: Synthesize and choose the most consistent answer relating triangle side lengths." , is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5 output: thinking - {thinking5.content}; answer - {answer5.content}")
    subtask_desc_5['response'] = {"thinking": thinking5, "answer": answer5}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_5)
    print("Step 5: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    reflect_inst_6 = "Given previous attempts and feedback, carefully consider where you could go wrong in your latest attempt. Using insights from previous attempts, try to solve the task better."
    cot_reflect_instruction_6 = "Sub-task 6: Derive algebraic equations linking the hexagon side length to the given triangle side lengths by combining the vector representations and the triangle side length relations." + reflect_inst_6
    subtask_desc_6 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_6",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_6,
        "context": ["user query", thinking4.content, thinking5.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }

    cot_inputs_6 = [taskInfo, thinking4, thinking5]

    thinking6, answer6 = await reflexion_cot_agent(cot_inputs_6, cot_reflect_instruction_6, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {reflexion_cot_agent.id}, deriving algebraic equations, thinking: {thinking6.content}; answer: {answer6.content}")

    for i in range(self.max_round):
        feedback6, correct6 = await reflexion_critic_agent([taskInfo, thinking6], "Please review and provide the limitations of provided solutions. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {reflexion_critic_agent.id}, feedback on algebraic derivation, thinking: {feedback6.content}; answer: {correct6.content}")
        if correct6.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_6.extend([thinking6, feedback6])
        thinking6, answer6 = await reflexion_cot_agent(cot_inputs_6, cot_reflect_instruction_6, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {reflexion_cot_agent.id}, refining algebraic equations, thinking: {thinking6.content}; answer: {answer6.content}")

    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 6 output: thinking - {thinking6.content}; answer - {answer6.content}")
    subtask_desc_6['response'] = {"thinking": thinking6, "answer": answer6}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_6)
    print("Step 6: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Stage 2

    cot_instruction_7 = "Sub-task 7: Solve the derived algebraic equations to find the numerical value of the hexagon's common side length, ensuring consistency with the convexity and parallelism constraints."
    subtask_desc_7 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_7",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_7,
        "context": ["user query", thinking6.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking7, answer7 = await cot_agent([taskInfo, thinking6], cot_instruction_7, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent.id}, solving algebraic equations, thinking: {thinking7.content}; answer: {answer7.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 7 output: thinking - {thinking7.content}; answer - {answer7.content}")
    subtask_desc_7['response'] = {"thinking": thinking7, "answer": answer7}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_7)
    print("Step 7: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    reflect_inst_8 = "Given previous attempts and feedback, carefully consider where you could go wrong in your latest attempt. Using insights from previous attempts, try to solve the task better."
    cot_reflect_instruction_8 = "Sub-task 8: Verify the solution by checking that the computed side length satisfies all geometric constraints and that the triangle side lengths correspond correctly to the given values." + reflect_inst_8
    subtask_desc_8 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_8",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_8,
        "context": ["user query", thinking7.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }

    cot_inputs_8 = [taskInfo, thinking7]

    thinking8, answer8 = await reflexion_cot_agent(cot_inputs_8, cot_reflect_instruction_8, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {reflexion_cot_agent.id}, verifying solution, thinking: {thinking8.content}; answer: {answer8.content}")

    for i in range(self.max_round):
        feedback8, correct8 = await reflexion_critic_agent([taskInfo, thinking8], "Please review and provide the limitations of provided verification. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {reflexion_critic_agent.id}, feedback on verification, thinking: {feedback8.content}; answer: {correct8.content}")
        if correct8.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_8.extend([thinking8, feedback8])
        thinking8, answer8 = await reflexion_cot_agent(cot_inputs_8, cot_reflect_instruction_8, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {reflexion_cot_agent.id}, refining verification, thinking: {thinking8.content}; answer: {answer8.content}")

    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 8 output: thinking - {thinking8.content}; answer - {answer8.content}")
    subtask_desc_8['response'] = {"thinking": thinking8, "answer": answer8}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_8)
    print("Step 8: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking8, answer8, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_instruction_1 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Formally define the geometric properties of the hexagon ABCDEF: establish that it is convex, equilateral (all sides equal), "
        "and that opposite sides are parallel, explicitly identifying the three pairs of opposite sides and their directions. Avoid assumptions about angles or coordinates at this stage."
    )
    cot_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent_1([taskInfo], cot_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_1.id}, defining hexagon properties, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    subtask_desc1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking1, "answer": answer1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_instruction_2 = (
        "Sub-task 2: Represent the hexagon sides as vectors in the plane, expressing the parallelism and equilateral conditions in vector form. "
        "Include the condition that the sum of the six side vectors is zero (polygon closure). Do not yet introduce offsets or distances from the origin."
    )
    cot_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc2 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }

    logs.append(subtask_desc2)

        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"

        thinking3, answer3 = await cot_agents_3[i]([taskInfo, thinking1], cot_sc_instruction_3, is_sub_task=True)

        possible_answers_3.append(answer3)
        possible_thinkings_3.append(thinking3)
    final_decision_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking3, answer3 = await final_decision_agent_3([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_3, "Sub-task 3: Synthesize and choose the most consistent answer for triangle construction." , is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}")

Let the vectors corresponding to sides AB, BC, CD, DE, EF, and FA be \\(\\vec{AB}, \\vec{BC}, \\vec{CD}, \\vec{DE}, \\vec{EF}, \\vec{FA}\\) respectively. Since the hexagon is equilateral, all these vectors have the same magnitude, say \\(s\\), the side length of the hexagon. The condition that opposite sides are parallel means that \\(\\vec{AB}\\) is parallel to \\(\\vec{DE}\\), \\(\\vec{BC}\\) is parallel to \\(\\vec{EF}\\), and \\(\\vec{CD}\\) is parallel to \\(\\vec{FA}\\). Parallel vectors differ by a scalar multiple, and since the sides are oriented consistently around the polygon, the opposite sides are parallel but point in opposite directions. Therefore, we can write \\(\\vec{DE} = -\\vec{AB}\\), \\(\\vec{EF} = -\\vec{BC}\\), and \\(\\vec{FA} = -\\vec{CD}\\). The polygon closure condition requires that the sum of all side vectors equals zero: \\(\\vec{AB} + \\vec{BC} + \\vec{CD} + \\vec{DE} + \\vec{EF} + \\vec{FA} = \\vec{0}\\).
